Dear Ritz-Carlton Pudong Management,

I hope this message finds you well. I am writing to express my extreme dissatisfaction with the service I received during my recent stay at your hotel from May 29 to May 30, 2024, in room 4323.

Upon checking out, I entrusted my luggage, including an Herm√®s Birkin 35 bag, to your porters while I went shopping. When I later retrieved my luggage and proceeded to the airport, I discovered once I was on the plane that my Herm√®s Birkin bag had been damaged. Specifically, there are two large black ink marks on the back of the bag. It appears that one of your employees caused these marks during the time they were responsible for my belongings.

This situation is unacceptable. I explicitly asked the porter who collected my luggage from the room to be careful with my Herm√®s bag as it is fragile. He assured me that he understood and would handle it with care. However, the resulting damage indicates a clear disregard for my instructions and the high standard of service I expected from a hotel of your reputation.

I am meticulous with my belongings and do not use pens, let alone carry them in my Herm√®s bag. The ink stains are permanent and irreparable, as I was informed when I purchased the bag. Additionally, the bag was in pristine condition upon my arrival at your hotel, throughout my stay, and at the time of checkout. Given that I used a luxury private chauffeur service to the airport and had the bag in my possession during the journey, it is evident that the damage occurred while the bag was in the hotel's custody.

I am deeply disappointed by the negligent service and have lost all confidence in your establishment. I have since returned to Paris and will consult with Herm√®s to explore any possible solutions, although I am not hopeful. The damaged Herm√®s Birkin 35 bag was a custom-made order, designed to my specifications, which took two years to receive. I have owned it for three years and maintained it in excellent condition.

Furthermore, I will be sharing this unfortunate experience with my network to caution them about the risks of staying at your hotel. Based on this incident, I will not recommend the Ritz-Carlton, nor any other Marriott properties, to anyone.

I am attaching photos of the damaged bag for your reference. Please be aware that I am considering legal action to seek compensation for the damage incurred.

Sincerely,
Constantin Ciorba

posted:Posted August 7, 2023
msg:Shanghai has been a city that I always travel to at least twice a year for as long as I remember, with that I have stayed at most of luxury hotels in this city. I can confidently say the Pudong Ritz-Carlton is one of the top. The service was amazing and definitely the star of the show. I came early and was awkwardly waiting in the lobby for my room, while waiting Vicky approached me to ask if I needed anything and then proceed to work with Ashin to get my room, a little after my room was just ready. So special thanks to the lobby people of Vicky and Ashin for the great service and help. 

The room was great - clean, large, elegant, with a lot of button controls. The facilities are pretty good, the gym has all the equipment you need and the pool is great - however the pool may be a little crowded later in the night. 

Mentioning service again, in my room I had a visit form a person bringing fruit as a welcome and also a gelato cart randomly showed up which I thought was amazing and hilarious, free ice cream anyone? Also I saw around noon to early afternoon check out rush hour the hotel brought a clown in for the kids, the guy made Ballons and stuff to entertain the lobby kids which could get a little rowdy sometimes, so that was great - the ice cream cart ended up in the lobby too. Little attention to details like that show that the hotel really care about its guests.

Another perk is the great views, from the hotel you can essentially see the whole puxi district of shanghai from south to north bund, the views are all around even in the gym. Also breakfast views were great. 

I will definitely come back when I get the chance, and thank you to Vicky and Ashin for all the care, even during rush hour where things may get a little hectic.

(2) The power socket on the bedside table is loose and can no longer charge electronic devices normally. The maintenance and inspection by the guest room engineering department is not in place. (3) The bathroom floor is paved with marble, but there is no "beware of slippery" sign visible to the naked eye. The floor is very slippery when wearing hotel slippers when it comes into contact with water. (4) There is a pervasive sewer smell in the bathroom. The hotel is relatively lacking in odor control and air optimization. Service: (1) The hotel's GSM and duty manager have a slow service pace, poor proactive service awareness, lack of communication skills, lack of empathy, and lack of skills in handling problems. (2) When faced with an emergency, the MOD and GSM did not communicate and apologize to the customer in the first place, which is aimed at maintaining the interests of the hotel and is contrary to your brand's consistent service concept. (3) During breakfast, a guest entered the dining area wearing the hotel's disposable slippers, and the hotel staff did not stop or remind them. In terms of the overall stay experience, the hotel has a superior location, and the service quality of the basic front-line staff is higher than that of the hotel's middle and senior management. Most employees will not take the initiative to greet guests in the public area, lack business etiquette, poor details, and need to improve their humanistic care. The overall service experience is average. Compared with other hotels of the same price and level, there is a big gap in hardware and software and room for improvement. I can only sigh that good employees have not met good leaders to lead them, resulting in poor connection between departments and poor customer experience. If you pursue service and quality, it is not recommended to choose the Pudong Ritz-Carlton. If you don't care about quality and experience for convenience, you can consider staying.

msg:I got the certificate with my boyfriend (now husband) and wanted to choose a hotel to celebrate and commemorate, and finally chose the Ritz. It turns out that my choice was correct, and the anniversary choice for the two of them is really good here!

Two days before the trip, a lady called to confirm the trip, and helped me to use the package benefits to upgrade the Pearl View Room and make an appoin**ent for the SPA time. I took the initiative to confirm with me whether it was a memorial day, and proposed a free arrangement. grateful.

Check in in the afternoon on the day of the trip, and the front desk is very polite. Although it was the first time, the unfamiliar environment did not create a sense of distance, and the experience was very good. Ashin from the Guest Recognition Depar**ent led us into the room and served with a smile throughout, thank you Ashin.

When I entered the room, I saw the elaborate arrangement of the Ritz, the balloons and the words Happy Wedding. The champagne in the package was iced, and a small dessert and welcome fruit were presented. There is also a handwritten letter, which is very caring and I like it very much, so it is also a beautiful souvenir to bring home.

I went swimming at night, probably because the temperature difference between indoor and outdoor is large at night, and the glass windows of the swimming pool are foggy and cannot enjoy the night view. The heated pool in the pool is very comfortable. The gym next to it is useless, but the view from the gym window is still great!

Breakfast in the morning, there are quite a lot of varieties, the small wontons are delicious, and the hotel's homemade yogurt is more impressive, and it tastes good. Having breakfast by the window overlooking Lujiazui is an unforgettable experience.

In the afternoon, I went to experience the Ritz SPA. Unexpectedly, the highest light of this journey turned out to be here. After taking a bath, wait in the women's lounge where you can drink tea, read newspapers, and have snacks. The SPA takes about 60 minutes, and it is very comfortable to fall asleep. Personally, I think it is slightly better than the experience of the SPA in Banyan Tree Huangshan. Until this time, I was really impressed by Ritz's service, impeccable.

Because the SPA waiting time was too long, which affected the check-out time, the front desk also helped to do a late check-out. When I left, I saw Filly, she arranged the room for us, thank you very much! Filly also gave us two room cards as souvenirs, which was really touching.

Although it was only two days, it made me feel the meticulous care and service, which left us with very good memories. I will consider coming to the Ritz on the anniversary in the future, thank you again!
